function getTemplateTabFromHoBMasters_() {

}

// âœ… ÎšÏÏÎ²ÎµÎ¹ Ï„Î¿ MASTER tab Î±Î½ Ï…Ï€Î¬ÏÏ‡Î¿Ï…Î½ Î¬Î»Î»Î± Î¿ÏÎ±Ï„Î¬
function hideLocalMasterIfVisible_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const masterSheet = ss.getSheetByName('MASTER');
if (masterSheet && !masterSheet.isSheetHidden()) {
const visibleSheets = ss.getSheets().filter(sh => !sh.isSheetHidden() && sh.getName() !== 'MASTER');
if (visibleSheets.length > 0) {
masterSheet.hideSheet();
}
}
}

function colorAllPlaceholdersB_(sheetName) {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
if (!sh) return;
const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
if (lastRow < 2) return;
const rng = sh.getRange(2, 2, lastRow - 1, 1);
const vals = rng.getValues();
const colors = rng.getFontColors();
const weights = rng.getFontWeights();

for (let i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
if (String(vals[i][0]).trim() === "ÎŒÎ½Î¿Î¼Î± Î•Ï€ÏÎ½Ï…Î¼Î¿?") {
colors[i][0] = "#d32f2f";
weights[i][0] = "bold";
}
}

rng.setFontColors(colors).setFontWeights(weights);
}

// âœ… Î‘Î½Ï„Î¹Î´ÏÎ¬ ÏƒÏ„Î¹Ï‚ Î±Î»Î»Î±Î³Î­Ï‚ Ï„Î·Ï‚ ÏƒÏ„Î®Î»Î·Ï‚ C (timestamp) Î® B (format)
function onEdit(e) {
try {
const sheet = e.range.getSheet();
const sheetName = sheet.getName();
const col = e.range.getColumn();
const row = e.range.getRow();
const val = e.range.getValue();

const excludedSheets = ["START", "MASTER"];
if (excludedSheets.includes(sheetName)) return;


const colB = 2, colC = 3, colD = 4;
const timestampFormat = 'HH:mm:ss.000" - "dd/MM';

if (col === colC) {
const cellB = sheet.getRange(row, colB);
if (!cellB.getValue()) {
cellB.setValue("ÎŒÎ½Î¿Î¼Î± Î•Ï€ÏÎ½Ï…Î¼Î¿?")
.setFontColor("#d32f2f")
.setFontWeight("bold");
}
const cellD = sheet.getRange(row, colD);
cellD.setNumberFormat(timestampFormat).setValue(new Date());
}

if (col === colB && val && val !== "ÎŒÎ½Î¿Î¼Î± Î•Ï€ÏÎ½Ï…Î¼Î¿?") {
e.range.setFontColor(null).setFontWeight(null).setBackground(null);
}
} catch (error) {

console.error("âŒ Î£Ï†Î¬Î»Î¼Î± ÏƒÏ„Î¿ onEdit:", error);
}
}

function getTemplateTabFromHoBMasters_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const fileName = ss.getName().trim(); // Ï€.Ï‡. GLYHOB, RENTIHOB

const masters = SpreadsheetApp.openById(HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID);
const tplSheet = masters.getSheetByName("Templates");
if (!tplSheet) return null;

const data = tplSheet.getRange(2, 1, tplSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
const [chkName, tplName] = data[i];
if (chkName && String(chkName).trim() === fileName) {
return tplName; // Ï€.Ï‡. MASTER1, MASTER2, WRHMaster
}
}
return null;
}

## /**

* Î”Î·Î¼Î¹Î¿Ï…ÏÎ³ÎµÎ¯ Î½Î­Î± Î·Î¼Î­ÏÎ± ÏƒÏ„Î¿ Î¤Î¡Î•Î§ÎŸÎ Î±ÏÏ‡ÎµÎ¯Î¿, Î±Î½Ï„Î¹Î³ÏÎ¬Ï†Î¿Î½Ï„Î±Ï‚ Ï„Î¿ template Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ HoB_Masters.

CashierMaster)

function createNewDay_AUTO(masterId, templateTab) {
var targetSS = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
var todayName = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, "dd/MM");

// Î‘Î½ Ï…Ï€Î¬ÏÏ‡ÎµÎ¹ Î®Î´Î· ÏƒÎ·Î¼ÎµÏÎ¹Î½ÏŒ tab â†’ ÎµÎ½Î·Î¼Î­ÏÏ‰ÏƒÎ· & Î­Î¾Î¿Î´Î¿Ï‚
var exists = targetSS.getSheetByName(todayName);
if (exists) {

try { PopupLib.showCustomPopup('â„¹ Î¥Ï€Î¬ÏÏ‡ÎµÎ¹ Î®Î´Î· Ï„Î¿ ÏƒÎ·Î¼ÎµÏÎ¹Î½ÏŒ TAB: <b>' + todayName + '</b>', 'info'); } catch
(_) {}
return;
}

// Î†Î½Î¿Î¹Î³Î¼Î± HoB_Masters ÎºÎ±Î¹ ÎµÏÏÎµÏƒÎ· template
var masters = SpreadsheetApp.openById(masterId);
var tpl = masters.getSheetByName(templateTab);
if (!tpl) {

try { PopupLib.showCustomPopup('âŒ Î”ÎµÎ½ Î²ÏÎ­Î¸Î·ÎºÎµ template "<b>' + templateTab + '</b>" ÏƒÏ„Î¿ HoB_Masters.',
'error'); } catch (_) {}
return;
}

// Copy Ï„Î¿Ï… template Î£Î¤ÎŸ Î•ÎÎ•Î¡Î“ÎŸ Î±ÏÏ‡ÎµÎ¯Î¿ & Î¼ÎµÏ„Î¿Î½Î¿Î¼Î±ÏƒÎ¯Î±
var newSheet = tpl.copyTo(targetSS).setName(todayName);

// ÎœÎµÏ„Î±ÎºÎ¯Î½Î·ÏƒÎ· Î¼Ï€ÏÎ¿ÏƒÏ„Î¬ (Î±ÏÎ¹ÏƒÏ„ÎµÏÎ¬) ÎºÎ±Î¹ Î¿ÏÎ¹ÏƒÎ¼ÏŒÏ‚ Ï‰Ï‚ ÎµÎ½ÎµÏÎ³ÏŒ
targetSS.setActiveSheet(newSheet);
targetSS.moveActiveSheet(0);

// Î ÏÎ¿Î±Î¹ÏÎµÏ„Î¹ÎºÎ¬: Î±Î½Ï„Î¹Î³ÏÎ±Ï†Î® protections Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ template
try {
// RANGE protections
var rps = tpl.getProtections(SpreadsheetApp.ProtectionType.RANGE) || [];
rps.forEach(function (p) {
try {
var r = p.getRange();
var p2 = newSheet.getRange(r.getA1Notation()).protect();
p2.setDescription(p.getDescription());


p2.setWarningOnly(p.isWarningOnly());
if (!p.isWarningOnly()) {
try { p2.removeEditors(p2.getEditors()); } catch (_) {}
var editors = p.getEditors();
if (editors && editors.length) p2.addEditors(editors);
try { if (p.canDomainEdit && p.canDomainEdit()) p2.setDomainEdit(true); } catch (_) {}
}
} catch (_) {}
});

// SHEET protection
var sps = tpl.getProtections(SpreadsheetApp.ProtectionType.SHEET) || [];
if (sps.length) {
try {
var sp = sps[0];
var sp2 = newSheet.protect();
sp2.setDescription(sp.getDescription());
sp2.setWarningOnly(sp.isWarningOnly());
if (!sp.isWarningOnly()) {
try { sp2.removeEditors(sp2.getEditors()); } catch (_) {}
var editors2 = sp.getEditors();
if (editors2 && editors2.length) sp2.addEditors(editors2);
try { if (sp.canDomainEdit && sp.canDomainEdit()) sp2.setDomainEdit(true); } catch (_) {}
}
} catch (_) {}
}
} catch (_) {}

// Stamp: Ï„ÎµÎ»ÎµÏ…Ï„Î±Î¯Î± Î´Î·Î¼Î¹Î¿Ï…ÏÎ³Î¯Î± tab (Î³Î¹Î± Î´Î¹ÎºÎ­Ï‚ ÏƒÎ¿Ï… ÏÎ¿Î­Ï‚/Î¼Î·Î½ÏÎ¼Î±Ï„Î±)
try {
PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties().setProperty('lastTabCreated', new Date().toISOString());
} catch (_) {}

try { PopupLib.showCustomPopup('âœ… Î”Î·Î¼Î¹Î¿Ï…ÏÎ³Î®Î¸Î·ÎºÎµ Ï„Î¿ ÏƒÎ·Î¼ÎµÏÎ¹Î½ÏŒ TAB: <b>' + todayName + '</b>', 'success'); }
catch (_) {}
}

function remindMissingNames() {
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
ss.getSheets().forEach(function (sheet) {
var name = sheet.getName();
if (name === "START" || name === "MASTER") return;

var last = sheet.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return;

var rng = sheet.getRange(2, 2, last - 1, 1);
var vals = rng.getValues();
var colors = rng.getFontColors();
var weights = rng.getFontWeights();
var bgs = rng.getBackgrounds();

for (var i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
var v = String(vals[i][0] || "").trim();
if (!v || v === "ÎŒÎ½Î¿Î¼Î± Î•Ï€ÏÎ½Ï…Î¼Î¿?") {

bgs[i][0] = "#ffebee";

function hideLocalMasterIfVisible_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const masterSheet = ss.getSheetByName('MASTER');
if (masterSheet && !masterSheet.isSheetHidden()) {
const visibleSheets = ss.getSheets().filter(sh => !sh.isSheetHidden() && sh.getName() !== 'MASTER');
if (visibleSheets.length > 0) {
masterSheet.hideSheet();
}
}
}

function hideLocalMasterIfVisible_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const masterSheet = ss.getSheetByName('MASTER');
if (!masterSheet) return;

// ÎˆÎ»ÎµÎ³Ï‡Î¿Ï‚ Î±Î½ Ï…Ï€Î¬ÏÏ‡ÎµÎ¹ ÏƒÎ·Î¼ÎµÏÎ¹Î½ÏŒ tab (Î® Î¿Ï€Î¿Î¹Î¿Î´Î®Ï€Î¿Ï„Îµ Î¬Î»Î»Î¿ ÎµÎºÏ„ÏŒÏ‚ MASTER)
const otherSheets = ss.getSheets().filter(sh => sh.getName() !== 'MASTER');
if (otherSheets.length > 0) {
masterSheet.hideSheet();
}

function showMasterAndDeleteOthers() {

## /**

*/
function remindMissingNames() {
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
ss.getSheets().forEach(function (sheet) {
var name = sheet.getName();
if (name === "START" || name === "MASTER") return;

var last = sheet.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return;

var rng = sheet.getRange(2, 2, last - 1, 1);
var vals = rng.getValues();
var colors = rng.getFontColors();
var weights = rng.getFontWeights();
var bgs = rng.getBackgrounds();

for (var i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
var v = String(vals[i][0] || "").trim();
if (!v || v === "ÎŒÎ½Î¿Î¼Î± Î•Ï€ÏÎ½Ï…Î¼Î¿?") {
colors[i][0] = "#d32f2f";
weights[i][0] = "bold";
bgs[i][0] = "#ffebee";
}
}
rng.setFontColors(colors).setFontWeights(weights).setBackgrounds(bgs);

function remindMissingNames() {
var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
ss.getSheets().forEach(function (sheet) {
var name = sheet.getName();
if (name === "START" || name === "MASTER") return;

var last = sheet.getLastRow();
if (last < 2) return;


var rng = sheet.getRange(2, 2, last - 1, 1);
var vals = rng.getValues();
var colors = rng.getFontColors();
var weights = rng.getFontWeights();
var bgs = rng.getBackgrounds();

for (var i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
var v = String(vals[i][0] || "").trim();
if (!v || v === "ÎŒÎ½Î¿Î¼Î± Î•Ï€ÏÎ½Ï…Î¼Î¿?") {
colors[i][0] = "#d32f2f";
weights[i][0] = "bold";
bgs[i][0] = "#ffebee";
}
}
rng.setFontColors(colors).setFontWeights(weights).setBackgrounds(bgs);
});

const HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID = '1j4xXEVYhVTzg57nhV-19V16F7AeoUjf6tJimFx4KOPI';
const MENU_SHEET_ID = '1JeDKj1CdWlAgPGnsRxCu2Fi1rkKxIBXeS861WXZDpEQ';
const MENU_SHEET_NAME = 'Menu';

// âœ… Î•Ï€Î¹ÏƒÏ„ÏÎ­Ï†ÎµÎ¹ email Î¹Î´Î¹Î¿ÎºÏ„Î®Ï„Î· (ÏŒÏ€Ï‰Ï‚ Ï„Î¿ Ï‡ÏÎ·ÏƒÎ¹Î¼Î¿Ï€Î¿Î¹ÎµÎ¯ Ï„Î¿ Checklist.gs)

// âœ… Î”Î¹Î±Î²Î¬Î¶ÎµÎ¹ menu entries Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ ÎµÎ¾Ï‰Ï„ÎµÏÎ¹ÎºÏŒ sheet "Menu".
// Î‘Î½Î±Î¼Î­Î½ÎµÎ¹ ÏƒÏ„Î®Î»ÎµÏ‚: [Store Name] | [Menu Name] | [Function Name] | [Type]
// ÏŒÏ€Î¿Ï… Type âˆˆ { 'user', 'owner' }
function getMenuItemsFromSheet(type) {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(MENU_SHEET_ID);
const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MENU_SHEET_NAME);
if (!sheet) return [];

// Î‘Î½Î¯Ï‡Î½ÎµÏ…ÏƒÎ· ÎµÏ€Î¹ÎºÎµÏ†Î±Î»Î¯Î´Ï‰Î½ ÎºÎ±Î¹ ÎµÏÏÎµÏƒÎ· ÏƒÏ„Î·Î»ÏÎ½
const header = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);
const idxStore = header.indexOf('Store Name') + 1;


const idxName = header.indexOf('Menu Name') + 1;
const idxFunc = header.indexOf('Function Name') + 1;
const idxType = header.indexOf('Type') + 1;

if (idxName === 0 || idxFunc === 0 || idxType === 0) return [];

const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
if (lastRow < 2) return [];

const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();

// Î¦Î¹Î»Ï„ÏÎ¬ÏÎ¿Ï…Î¼Îµ Î¼Îµ Î²Î¬ÏƒÎ· Ï„Î¿ type (user/owner). Î¤Î¿ Store Name Ï€ÏÎ¿Ï‚ Ï„Î¿ Ï€Î±ÏÏŒÎ½ Î´ÎµÎ½ Ï„Î¿ Ï†Î¹Î»Ï„ÏÎ¬ÏÎ¿Ï…Î¼Îµ.
const items = [];
data.forEach(row => {
const store = idxStore? row[idxStore - 1] : '';
const name = row[idxName - 1];
const func = row[idxFunc - 1];
const rtype = row[idxType - 1];

if (String(rtype).trim().toLowerCase() === String(type).trim().toLowerCase()
&& name && func) {
items.push({ store: store || 'ALL', name: String(name), func: String(func), type: String(rtype) });
}
});

return items;
}

// ğŸ”ğŸ” Helper â€” FULL DYNAMIC Template Lookup (Î¯Î´Î¹Î± Î»Î¿Î³Î¹ÎºÎ® Î¼Îµ Checklist.gs)
// ==========================
function getTemplateTabFromHoBMasters_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const fileName = ss.getName().trim();

const masters = SpreadsheetApp.openById(HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID);
const tplSheet = masters.getSheetByName('Templates');
if (!tplSheet) return null;

const data = tplSheet.getRange(2, 1, tplSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
const chkName = data[i][0];
const tplName = data[i][1];
if (chkName && String(chkName).trim() === fileName) {
return tplName; // Ï€.Ï‡. MASTER1 / MASTER2 / WRHMaster / EshopMaster / CashierMaster
}
}
return null;
}

// âœ… Helper: Î†Î½Î¿Î¹Î³Î¼Î± URL ÏƒÎµ Dialog
// ==========================
function openUrlInDialog(url, title) {
var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput('<iframe src="' + url + '" width="100%" height="100%"></iframe>')
.setWidth(1000)
.setHeight(600);
SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, title);
}

// ==========================
// HoB - Menu Library (V6.6) â€” Owner & User Menu


// Owner Tools: AdminToolsLib
// User Tools: Links Î±Î½Î¿Î¯Î³Î¿Ï…Î½ ÏƒÎµ Î½Î­Î¿ browser tab
// ==========================

// âœ… IDs (Î¯Î´Î¹Î± Î¼Îµ Ï„Î± Ï…Ï€ÏŒÎ»Î¿Î¹Ï€Î± Î±ÏÏ‡ÎµÎ¯Î± ÏƒÎ¿Ï… )
const HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID = '1j4xXEVYhVTzg57nhV-19V16F7AeoUjf6tJimFx4KOPI';
const MENU_SHEET_ID = '1JeDKj1CdWlAgPGnsRxCu2Fi1rkKxIBXeS861WXZDpEQ';
const MENU_SHEET_NAME = 'Menu';

// âœ… Î•Ï€Î¹ÏƒÏ„ÏÎ­Ï†ÎµÎ¹ email Î¹Î´Î¹Î¿ÎºÏ„Î®Ï„Î·
function getOwnerEmail() {
return 'hobdeks@gmail.com';
}

// âœ… Î”Î¹Î±Î²Î¬Î¶ÎµÎ¹ menu entries Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ ÎµÎ¾Ï‰Ï„ÎµÏÎ¹ÎºÏŒ sheet "Menu"
function getMenuItemsFromSheet(type) {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(MENU_SHEET_ID);
const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MENU_SHEET_NAME);
if (!sheet) return [];

const header = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);
const idxStore = header.indexOf('Store Name') + 1;
const idxName = header.indexOf('Menu Name') + 1;
const idxFunc = header.indexOf('Function Name') + 1;
const idxType = header.indexOf('Type') + 1;
if (idxName === 0 || idxFunc === 0 || idxType === 0) return [];

const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
if (lastRow < 2) return [];

const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
const items = [];
data.forEach(row => {
const store = idxStore? row[idxStore - 1] : '';
const name = row[idxName - 1];
const func = row[idxFunc - 1];
const rtype = row[idxType - 1];
if (String(rtype).trim().toLowerCase() === String(type).trim().toLowerCase()
&& name && func) {
items.push({ store: store || 'ALL', name: String(name), func: String(func), type: String(rtype) });
}
});
return items;
}

// Helper â€” FULL DYNAMIC Template Lookup
// ==========================
function getTemplateTabFromHoBMasters_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const fileName = ss.getName().trim();

const masters = SpreadsheetApp.openById(HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID);
const tplSheet = masters.getSheetByName('Templates');
if (!tplSheet) return null;

const data = tplSheet.getRange(2, 1, tplSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
const chkName = data[i][0];
const tplName = data[i][1];
if (chkName && String(chkName).trim() === fileName) {
return tplName;
}
}
return null;
}

// ==========================
// HoB - Menu Library (V6.7) â€” Owner & User Menu
// Owner Tools: AdminToolsLib
// User Tools: Links Î±Î½Î¿Î¯Î³Î¿Ï…Î½ Î¬Î¼ÎµÏƒÎ± ÏƒÎµ Î½Î­Î¿ browser tab

// âœ… IDs
const HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID = '1j4xXEVYhVTzg57nhV-19V16F7AeoUjf6tJimFx4KOPI';
const MENU_SHEET_ID = '1JeDKj1CdWlAgPGnsRxCu2Fi1rkKxIBXeS861WXZDpEQ';
const MENU_SHEET_NAME = 'Menu';

// âœ… Î•Ï€Î¹ÏƒÏ„ÏÎ­Ï†ÎµÎ¹ email Î¹Î´Î¹Î¿Îº Ï„Î®Ï„Î·
function getOwnerEmail() {

// âœ… Î”Î¹Î±Î²Î¬Î¶ÎµÎ¹ menu entries Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ ÎµÎ¾Ï‰Ï„ÎµÏÎ¹ÎºÏŒ sheet "Menu"
function getMenuItemsFromSheet(type) {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(MENU_SHEET_ID);
const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MENU_SHEET_NAME);
if (!sheet) return [];

const header = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);
const idxStore = header.indexOf('Store Name') + 1;
const idxName = header.indexOf('Menu Name') + 1;
const idxFunc = header.indexOf('Function Name') + 1;
const idxType = header.indexOf('Type') + 1;


if (idxName === 0 || idxFunc === 0 || idxType === 0) return [];

const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
if (lastRow < 2) return [];

const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
const items = [];
data.forEach(row => {
const store = idxStore? row[idxStore - 1] : '';
const name = row[idxName - 1];
const func = row[idxFunc - 1];
const rtype = row[idxType - 1];
if (String(rtype).trim().toLowerCase() === String(type).trim().toLowerCase()
&& name && func) {
items.push({ store: store || 'ALL', name: String(name), func: String(func), type: String(rtype) });
}
});
return items;
}

return;

} catch (err) {
PopupLib.showCustomPopup('âš  Î£Ï†Î¬Î»Î¼Î± (Create New Day):<br><br>' + (err.message || err), 'error');
}
}

// Helper: Î†Î½Î¿Î¹Î³Î¼Î± URL ÏƒÎµ Î½Î­Î¿ tab (Ï‡Ï‰ÏÎ¯Ï‚ popup Î¼Î®Î½Ï…Î¼Î±)
// ==========================
function openUrlInNewTab(url) {
var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(
"<script>window.open('" + url + "', '_blank');</script>"
);
SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModelessDialog(html, "");
}

// ==========================
// Helper â€” FULL DYNAMIC Template Lookup
// ==========================
function getTemplateTabFromHoBMasters_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const fileName = ss.getName().trim();

const masters = SpreadsheetApp.openById(HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID);
const tplSheet = masters.getSheetByName('Templates');
if (!tplSheet) return null;

const data = tplSheet.getRange(2, 1, tplSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
const chkName = data[i][0];
const tplName = data[i][1];
if (chkName && String(chkName).trim() === fileName) {
return tplName;
}
}
return null;
}

// ==========================
// HoB - Menu Library (V6.8) â€” Owner & User Menu

// âœ… IDs
const HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID = '1j4xXEVYhVTzg57nhV-19V16F7AeoUjf6tJimFx4KOPI';
const MENU_SHEET_ID = '1JeDKj1CdWlAgPGnsRxCu2Fi1rkKxIBXeS861WXZDpEQ';
const MENU_SHEET_NAME = 'Menu';

// âœ… Î•Ï€Î¹ÏƒÏ„ÏÎ­Ï†ÎµÎ¹ email Î¹Î´Î¹Î¿ÎºÏ„Î®Ï„Î·
function getOwnerEmail() {

// âœ… Î”Î¹Î±Î²Î¬Î¶ÎµÎ¹ menu entries Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ ÎµÎ¾Ï‰Ï„ÎµÏÎ¹ÎºÏŒ sheet "Menu"
function getMenuItemsFromSheet(type) {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(MENU_SHEET_ID);
const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MENU_SHEET_NAME);
if (!sheet) return [];

const header = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);
const idxStore = header.indexOf('Store Name') + 1;
const idxName = header.indexOf('Menu Name') + 1;
const idxFunc = header.indexOf('Function Name') + 1;
const idxType = header.indexOf('Type') + 1;
if (idxName === 0 || idxFunc === 0 || idxType === 0) return [];

const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
if (lastRow < 2) return [];

const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
const items = [];
data.forEach(row => {
const store = idxStore? row[idxStore - 1] : '';
const name = row[idxName - 1];
const func = row[idxFunc - 1];
const rtype = row[idxType - 1];
if (String(rtype).trim().toLowerCase() === String(type).trim().toLowerCase()
&& name && func) {
items.push({ store: store || 'ALL', name: String(name), func: String(func), type: String(rtype) });
}
});
return items;
}

// Helper: Î†Î½Î¿Î¹Î³Î¼Î± URL ÏƒÎµ Î½Î­Î¿ tab (Ï‡Ï‰ÏÎ¯Ï‚ errors)
// ==========================
function openUrlInNewTab(url) {
var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(
"<script>window.open('" + url + "', '_blank');google.script.host.close();</script>"
);
SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModelessDialog(html, "Î†Î½Î¿Î¹Î³Î¼Î±"); // <-- ÎµÎ»Î¬Ï‡Î¹ÏƒÏ„Î¿Ï‚ Ï„Î¯Ï„Î»Î¿Ï‚, Î±Ï€Î¿Ï†ÎµÏÎ³ÎµÎ¹ error
}

// ==========================
// Helper â€” FULL DYNAMIC Template Lookup


## // ==========================

function getTemplateTabFromHoBMasters_() {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const fileName = ss.getName().trim();

const masters = SpreadsheetApp.openById(HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID);
const tplSheet = masters.getSheetByName('Templates');
if (!tplSheet) return null;

const data = tplSheet.getRange(2, 1, tplSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
const chkName = data[i][0];
const tplName = data[i][1];
if (chkName && String(chkName).trim() === fileName) {
return tplName;
}
}
return null;
}

function createNewDay_AUTO(hobMastersFileId, templateTab) {
try {

const tpl = master.getSheetByName(templateTab);
if (!tpl) throw new Error("Î”ÎµÎ½ Î²ÏÎ­Î¸Î·ÎºÎµ template: " + templateTab);

const copy = tpl.copyTo(ss);
copy.setName(new Date().toLocaleDateString("el-GR"));

ss.moveActiveSheet(1);

// ÎšÏÏÎ²Î¿Ï…Î¼Îµ Ï„Î¿ MASTER Î³Î¹Î± Î½Î± Î¼Î· Î´Î¿Ï…Î»ÎµÏÎ¿Ï…Î½ Ï‡ÏÎ®ÏƒÏ„ÎµÏ‚ Ï€Î¬Î½Ï‰ Ï„Î¿Ï…

if (masterSheet && !masterSheet.isSheetHidden()) {
masterSheet.hideSheet();
}

PopupLib.showCustomPopup("âœ… Î”Î·Î¼Î¹Î¿Ï…ÏÎ³Î®Î¸Î·ÎºÎµ Î½Î­Î± Î·Î¼Î­ÏÎ± Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ template <b>" + templateTab + "</b>.",
"success");

}
}

// ğŸ“ŒğŸ“Œ Duplicate & Cleanup
// ==========================
function automatedDuplicateAndCleanup() {
try {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
const sheets = ss.getSheets();
const master = sheets.find(sh => sh.getName().toUpperCase() === "MASTER");
if (!master) throw new Error("Î”ÎµÎ½ Î²ÏÎ­Î¸Î·ÎºÎµ MASTER");

// Î”Î¹Î±Î³ÏÎ±Ï†Î® ÏŒÎ»Ï‰Î½ Ï„Ï‰Î½ Î¬Î»Î»Ï‰Î½ tabs
sheets.forEach(sh => {
if (sh.getName() !== "MASTER") ss.deleteSheet(sh);
});

// Î•Ï€Î±Î½ÎµÎ¼Ï†Î¬Î½Î¹ÏƒÎ· MASTER
if (master.isSheetHidden()) master.showSheet();

PopupLib.showCustomPopup("â™» ÎˆÎ³Î¹Î½Îµ Duplicate & Cleanup (ÎºÏÎ±Ï„Î®Î¸Î·ÎºÎµ Î¼ÏŒÎ½Î¿ Ï„Î¿ MASTER).", "info");
} catch (err) {

PopupLib.showCustomPopup("âš  Î£Ï†Î¬Î»Î¼Î± (Duplicate & Cleanup):<br><br>" + (err.message || err), "error");
}
}

// (Î ÏÎ¿Î±Î¹ÏÎµÏ„Î¹ÎºÏŒ) Blinking Helper
// ==========================
function blinkCellFontColor_(cells, cycles) {
for (let i = 0; i < cycles; i++) {
cells.forEach(cell => cell.setFontColor("red"));
SpreadsheetApp.flush();
Utilities.sleep(250);
cells.forEach(cell => cell.setFontColor("black"));
SpreadsheetApp.flush();
Utilities.sleep(250);
}
}

function remindMissingNames() {

if (last < 2) return;

// ==========================
// (Î ÏÎ¿Î±Î¹ÏÎµÏ„Î¹ÎºÏŒ) Blinking Helper
// ==========================
function blinkCellFontColor_(cells, cycles) {
for (var i = 0; i < cycles; i++) {
cells.forEach(function(cell){ cell.setFontColor("red"); });
SpreadsheetApp.flush(); Utilities.sleep(250);
cells.forEach(function(cell){ cell.setFontColor("black"); });
SpreadsheetApp.flush(); Utilities.sleep(250);
}
}

function automatedDuplicateAndCleanup() {

var newName = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), tz, "dd/MM") + " Copy";

var newSheet = activeSheet.copyTo(ss).setName(newName);
newSheet.getDataRange().clearNotes().clearFormat().setFontWeight("normal");

âœ… **ÎŸÎ»Î¿ÎºÎ»Î·ÏÏ‰Î¼Î­Î½Î¿Ï‚ ÎµÎ½Î·Î¼ÎµÏÏ‰Î¼Î­Î½Î¿Ï‚ MenuLib (Î¼Îµ Ï„Î¹Ï‚ Î½Î­ÎµÏ‚ Ï€ÏÎ¿ÏƒÎ¸Î®ÎºÎµÏ‚)**
// ==========================
// HoB - Menu Library (V6.9) â€” Owner & User Menu
// Owner Tools: AdminToolsLib
// User Tools: Links Î±Î½Î¿Î¯Î³Î¿Ï…Î½ Î¬Î¼ÎµÏƒÎ± ÏƒÎµ Î½Î­Î¿ browser tab

// âœ… IDs
const HOB_MASTERS_FILE_ID = '1j4xXEVYhVTzg57nhV-19V16F7AeoUjf6tJimFx4KOPI';

// âœ… Î•Ï€Î¹ÏƒÏ„ÏÎ­Ï†ÎµÎ¹ email Î¹Î´Î¹Î¿ÎºÏ„Î®Ï„Î·


function getOwnerEmail() {

// âœ… Î”Î¹Î±Î²Î¬Î¶ÎµÎ¹ menu entries Î±Ï€ÏŒ Ï„Î¿ ÎµÎ¾Ï‰Ï„ÎµÏÎ¹ÎºÏŒ sheet "Menu"
function getMenuItemsFromSheet(type) {
const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(MENU_SHEET_ID);
const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MENU_SHEET_NAME);
if (!sheet) return [];

const header = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);
const idxStore = header.indexOf('Store Name') + 1;
const idxName = header.indexOf('Menu Name') + 1;
const idxFunc = header.indexOf('Function Name') + 1;
const idxType = header.indexOf('Type') + 1;
if (idxName === 0 || idxFunc === 0 || idxType === 0) return [];

const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
if (lastRow < 2) return [];

const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
const items = [];
data.forEach(row => {
const store = idxStore? row[idxStore - 1] : '';
const name = row[idxName - 1];
const func = row[idxFunc - 1];
const rtype = row[idxType - 1];
if (String(rtype).trim().toLowerCase() === String(type).trim().toLowerCase()
&& name && func) {
items.push({ store: store || 'ALL', name: String(name), func: String(func), type: String(rtype) });
}
});
return items;
}
